Plus, I use the wave clips instead of the roller clips that come with the steamer (wave clips are usually silver, and I found a set of 12 on the hair and beauty aisle at my local grocery store). The roller clips leave creases, whereas the wave clips don't and allow the hair to dry faster. RECOMMENDATION: When setting the hair, try using a little moisturizer or shine gel on the ends. My hair usually doesn't frizz, but after using the steam rollers, the ends frizzed a little; I assume it was because of the steam. Rubbing a little bit of shine gel on the ends before rolling my hair solved the problem. My only criticism: you can only enjoy this product if you actually get it in working order! The first time I ordered it, the post that holds the rollerin place on the steam unit was broken off. Plus, the steam unit wasn't functioning properly. To Amazon's credit, they overnighted a replacement at no further cost to me. Unfortunately, the post on THAT one was broken too! Plus, neither one had the right mix of rollers in them! It says it comes with 6 each of petite, small, medium, large, and jumbo rollers, but neither package contained any large rollers at all. VERY irritating!   159. I think this is a great product! My hair is to the middle of my back and very thick. My hair always feels so soft and healthy after using these! With other rollers, I have to use at least 20 large or jumbo rollers and they never give you enough so I have to buy two hot roller units. I did have to order some extra jumbo rollers with this steam setter (which was no big deal), but I only have to use 12 rollers which makes it quicker and easier and the curls come out perfect. I don't mind that it comes with a variety of sizes that you may not use because I may decide to get creative with my hair one day and use them! I just keep the ones that I don't use and the instruction manual in the original box and I keep the unit and the ones that I do use in the bag that comes with it within easier reach. I will say that I do have to leave the rollers on the steamer longer than it says (I do 20 to 25 seconds), and I also steam the clip. I also, just for extra hold and to save time, I run a hot blow dryer over the curlers (but not enough to damage), then put it on cool and cool it off and dry for a couple of minutes being sure to get in between the curlers. I can usually take them out immediately. Some people don't like that it only steams one at a time. I don't really mind it so much. The best way to do it to save time after you have sectioned your hair into the main sections is: 1. Put the roller on the steamer while you are getting a section of hair to roll and combing it out to make it smooth (just take your time so it has plenty of time to steam and count to 20 or so). 2. While holding the hair to be rolled with one hand, use your other hand to pick up the roller off the steamer and then put a clip onto the steamer that will steam while you are rolling. Then roll the hair. 3. While you are holding the rolled curl with one hand, use your other hand to pick up the clip off the steamer and put on another curler to start steaming for your next curl. Then put the clip over the roller. 4. Start getting your next section of hair ready to roll while the roller is on the steamer and continue to follow the above pattern. This way, not much time is wasted waiting for rollers to steam!

You will need hair spray to set the look.   255. I had my doubts when I was considering whether to buy this roller. It takes practice and experience to know what gives you the best results. I have straight, dyed, medium fine hair. It was a little tricky to use at first, I didn't know how long to heat each roller, or how long to leave it in. Different reviews said different things. I was confused...as many of you probably are now..<br /><br />I have learned that the curls stay in my hair longest when I do not oversteam the rollers(I use it on normal setting, not the ionic) First, I put the roller on the steamer, and then I proceed to take a small section of my hair. By the time I have a section of hair ready to be curled onto the roller, the roller is done steaming. I would estimate that to be about 5 seconds. After I remove the roller from the steamer, I put the cap on the steamer for it to steam. And once I am done rolling my hair onto the roller, I take the heated cover, put it onto my rolled hair. This process is pretty quick.<br /><br />If I leave the roller on the steamer longer than 10 seconds, the rollers might be too wet. You will know if it is too wet when you remove the rollers from your hair and realize that your hair is semi-damp. This way, the curls will not stay. You might try to salvage it by blow drying it. But better to have steamed rollers than wet rollers in the first place.<br /><br />If you want the curls to remain all day, you will need hair spray. I do not use hair spray because I like the relaxed and wavy curled look. This will depend on how you want it.<br /><br />I prefer this steamer so much more than the curling iron. The curling iron is just so damaging. I don't believe in using heat protectant either. Hence, this set works well for me, now I can curls whenver I want without thinking about the damage it would do to my hair!<br /><br />The ionic setting DOES give out a loud clicking noise, and it is stated on the manual that the unit will click. However, I use this on the normal steam setting, and it works just as fine. You don't necessarily need the ionic setting to achieve the curls you desire. Though I hasten myself to say that I do get annoyed with the clicking noise.<br /><br />Overall, great steamer set to have if you have some perverse feelings or ideas towards the hot curling iron. I would definitely repurchase this if I had to. Enjoy!

  287. These are the BEST steam rollers I have ever used! But I think any steam rollers would do great. I have been using it for over 15 years. The key to keeping the full, bouncy curls when it's humid is using a thermal styling spray before rolling up your hair on it. I like Redken's 22 Hot sets and Kenra's Thermal styling spray 19 or 20. ( I think 20 smells better.) You can get those anywhere now, even at Walmart or Amazon. I have long fine hair. To cut down on my time, I dry my hair completely using a great brush, and spray my hair lightly with setting spray, pulling my hair up and such to get different layers. Then I shoot it with the dryer and comb out. Remember, I said lightly. Then, i pull my hair up in a pony tail (you will have to experiment height and placement on your own) and I use two jumbo rollers. Splitting my pony tail in half, I comb through one half, spray lightly on both sides, comb through to keep from the hair matting once rolled, and I let the steam go in roller for about 10 seconds since my hair is long(past my shoulders by 2 inches maybe more) Your hair has to get hot then cool off to set. This is what a beautician told me. I roll my long bangs but I do not put a cover over it, I lean over and steam the bangs in the roller then let cool for a few seconds, blast with heat, then with cool setting and unroll like a ringlet. Once I roll my pony tail, I let set for a few minutes while putting on my make up. I also steam the inside of cover before I put it on the roller I have my hair rolled up on. I have rolled my hair this way for 25 years before I started steam rollers. I have not set the rollers all over my head because with 3 boys and work, I don't have time but the last time I did it turned out with tighter curls. Thermal setting spray is key and mousse sometimes is great for more body. I have experimented with different sizes of rollers for different sized curls. It's your preference and it may take a few times to get the look you want...everyone's hair is DIFFERENT, but after being in 7 weddings in one year, in Austin, Texas, during the lovely humid and hot summer months, THERMAL SETTING SPRAY and Anti-humidity hair spray are your BEST FRIENDS!u want...everyone's hair is DIFFERENT, but after being in 7 weddings in one year, in Austin, Texas, during the lovely humid and hot summer months, THERMAL SETTING SPRAY and Anti-humidity hair spray are your BEST FRIENDS!

The great part about it is that so many rollers of different sizes were in the set, and we all have different hair lengths, making it easy for all of us to have rollers in our hair at the same time if we need to. And to those with african american hair that have complained of frizziness, I have found that lightly using a little coconut oil with my olive oil setting foam and end papers works wonders for preventing the frizz. Also, I've found that different steam times for each size roller are much more effective, i.e. shorter steaming time (5 or 6 seconds) for small or petite rollers while longer (like 9 to 11 seconds) for jumbo rollers. If you allow the roller to become soaked the drying process will become much longer, and you increase the risk for frizz. If you're looking for something that's quick and don't mind a styling method that will actually condition your hair at the same time, I think this steamer is the way to go.<br /><br />By the way, I VERY RARELY review anything... ever...but I felt the world should know about this since, apparently, I was super late :)<br /><br />Have fun with your steam hairsetters guys!!!

  377. The website states &#34;The only patented steam hair setting sytem with worldwide dual voltage.&#34; But this is not the case! The device and the manual both clearly say 120V only...meaning folks in Asia, Australia and Europe cannot use this product without a current converter (not just an adapter plug). Additionally, the plug is a polarised plug, meaning that one end is fatter than the other (not just a standard US plug) and may not work with your normal travel adapters....<br /><br />Buying a current converter is not necessarily cheap, especially if you are ordering online as these things are heavy and shipping will be expensive. This is a consideration to bear in mind if you are hell-bent on using this product.<br /><br />The product looks fine and has a great reputation from users, but it's a shame that I can't tell you personally how good it is because of the website's blatant misrepresentation. Ebay sellers may also have copied the description and will be subject to the same misrep problem...someone should really fix the description!
